Compute stress following small deformation elasticity

  • computeTrueWhen false, MOOSE will not call compute methods on this material. The user must call computeProperties() after retrieving the MaterialBase via MaterialBasePropertyInterface::getMaterialBase(). Non-computed MaterialBases are not sorted for dependencies.

    Default:True

    C++ Type:bool

    Options:

    Description:When false, MOOSE will not call compute methods on this material. The user must call computeProperties() after retrieving the MaterialBase via MaterialBasePropertyInterface::getMaterialBase(). Non-computed MaterialBases are not sorted for dependencies.

  • constant_onNONEWhen ELEMENT, MOOSE will only call computeQpProperties() for the 0th quadrature point, and then copy that value to the other qps.When SUBDOMAIN, MOOSE will only call computeSubdomainProperties() for the 0th quadrature point, and then copy that value to the other qps. Evaluations on element qps will be skipped

    Default:NONE

    C++ Type:MooseEnum

    Options:NONE ELEMENT SUBDOMAIN

    Description:When ELEMENT, MOOSE will only call computeQpProperties() for the 0th quadrature point, and then copy that value to the other qps.When SUBDOMAIN, MOOSE will only call computeSubdomainProperties() for the 0th quadrature point, and then copy that value to the other qps. Evaluations on element qps will be skipped

  • elastic_energy_nameE_elname of the material that holds the elastic energy

    Default:E_el

    C++ Type:MaterialPropertyName

    Options:

    Description:name of the material that holds the elastic energy

  • extra_stress_namesMaterial property names of rank two tensors to be added to the stress.

    C++ Type:std::vector

    Options:

    Description:Material property names of rank two tensors to be added to the stress.

examples/mud_quasi1D_analytical/script_varying_L_Eratio_20/run2/fracture.i

[GlobalParams]
  displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = 'geo.msh'
[]

[Variables]
  [./d]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
  [../]
  [./bounds_dummy]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
[]

[Bounds]
  [./nonnegtivity]
    type = BoundsAux
    variable = bounds_dummy
    bounded_variable = d
    upper = 1
    lower = 0
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./damage]
    type = PhaseFieldFractureEvolution
    variable = d
    driving_energy_name = E_el
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_film]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_substrate]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 8.333333E+01
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./stress_substrate]
    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_film]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.973835E-04'
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_substrate]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.973835E+00'
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_film]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 2.511886E-02
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_substrate]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 2.511886E-02
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -snes_type'
  petsc_options_value = 'lu vinewtonrsls'
  dt = 6.835231E-06

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-06
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
[]
Close

examples/mud_quasi1D_analytical/script_varying_L_Eratio_0.5/run6/fracture.i

[GlobalParams]

  [../]
  [./bounds_dummy]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
[]

    type = BoundsAux
    variable = bounds_dummy
    bounded_variable = d
    upper = 1
    lower = 0
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./damage]
    type = PhaseFieldFractureEvolution
    variable = d
    driving_energy_name = E_el
  [../]

    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is

    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]

    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 2.083333E+00

  [../]

    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]

    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'

    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.055164E-04'
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_substrate]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'

examples/mud_quasi1D_analytical/script_varying_L_Eratio_2/run11/mechanical.i

[GlobalParams]
  displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = 'geo.msh'
[]

[MultiApps]
  [./fracture]
    type = TransientMultiApp
    input_files = 'fracture.i'
    app_type = raccoonApp
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
[]

[Transfers]
  [./disp_x]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_x'
    variable = 'disp_x'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_y'
    variable = 'disp_y'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd_ref'
    variable = 'd_ref'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = from_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd'
    variable = 'd'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./load]
    type = MultiAppScalarToAuxScalarTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'load'
    to_aux_scalar = 'load'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./boundary_xdisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./boundary_ydisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./Periodic]
    [./disp_x]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '2.511886E+01 0 0'
    [../]
    [./disp_y]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '2.511886E+01 0 0'
    [../]
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_film]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_substrate]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 8.333333E+00
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./stress_substrate]
    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_film]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '4.859951E-04'
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_substrate]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '4.859951E+00'
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_film]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 2.511886E-01
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_substrate]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 2.511886E-01
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Postprocessors]
  [./fracture_energy]
    type = FractureEnergy
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = TransientSupNorm
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  dt = 4.499979E-06

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load fracture_energy'
  exodus = true
  print_linear_residuals = false
[]
Close

[GlobalParams]

  type = FileMesh
  file = 'geo.msh'
[]

[MultiApps]
  [./fracture]
    type = TransientMultiApp
    input_files = 'fracture.i'
    app_type = raccoonApp
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
[]

[Transfers]
  [./disp_x]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_x'
    variable = 'disp_x'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_y'
    variable = 'disp_y'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd_ref'
    variable = 'd_ref'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = from_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd'
    variable = 'd'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]

examples/mud_quasi1D_analytical/script_varying_L_Eratio_10/run6/mechanical.i

[GlobalParams]
  displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = 'geo.msh'
[]

[MultiApps]
  [./fracture]
    type = TransientMultiApp
    input_files = 'fracture.i'
    app_type = raccoonApp
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
[]

[Transfers]
  [./disp_x]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_x'
    variable = 'disp_x'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_y'
    variable = 'disp_y'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd_ref'
    variable = 'd_ref'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = from_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd'
    variable = 'd'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./load]
    type = MultiAppScalarToAuxScalarTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'load'
    to_aux_scalar = 'load'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
[]

  [../]

  [../]

    component = 0
  [../]
  [./solid_y]

    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
  [../]
[]

    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]

    variable = disp_y
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]

    [./disp_x]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '3.162278E+00 0 0'
    [../]
    [./disp_y]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '3.162278E+00 0 0'
    [../]
  [../]

    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]

    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_substrate]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 8.333333E+02
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./stress_substrate]
    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]

    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.973835E-04'
    block = 'film'

  [../]

    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_film]
    type = FractureMaterial

    L = 3.162278E-02

    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_substrate]

examples/mud_quasi1D_analytical/script_varying_L_Eratio_20/run7/mechanical.i

[GlobalParams]
  displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = 'geo.msh'
[]

[MultiApps]
  [./fracture]
    type = TransientMultiApp
    input_files = 'fracture.i'
    app_type = raccoonApp
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
[]

[Transfers]
  [./disp_x]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_x'
    variable = 'disp_x'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_y'
    variable = 'disp_y'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd_ref'
    variable = 'd_ref'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = from_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd'
    variable = 'd'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./load]
    type = MultiAppScalarToAuxScalarTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'load'
    to_aux_scalar = 'load'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./boundary_xdisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./boundary_ydisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./Periodic]
    [./disp_x]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '4.466836E+00 0 0'
    [../]
    [./disp_y]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '4.466836E+00 0 0'
    [../]
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_film]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_substrate]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 8.333333E+01
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./stress_substrate]
    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_film]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.973835E-04'
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_substrate]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.973835E+00'
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_film]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 4.466836E-02
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_substrate]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 4.466836E-02
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Postprocessors]
  [./fracture_energy]
    type = FractureEnergy
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = TransientSupNorm
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  dt = 5.893127E-06

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load fracture_energy'
  exodus = true
  print_linear_residuals = false
[]

examples/mud_quasi1D_analytical/script_varying_L_Eratio_20/run11/mechanical.i

[GlobalParams]
  displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = 'geo.msh'
[]

[MultiApps]
  [./fracture]
    type = TransientMultiApp
    input_files = 'fracture.i'
    app_type = raccoonApp
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
[]

[Transfers]
  [./disp_x]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_x'
    variable = 'disp_x'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_y'
    variable = 'disp_y'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd_ref'
    variable = 'd_ref'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = from_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd'
    variable = 'd'

examples/mud_quasi1D_analytical/script_varying_L_Eratio_10/run7/mechanical.i

[GlobalParams]
  displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = 'geo.msh'
[]

[MultiApps]
  [./fracture]
    type = TransientMultiApp
    input_files = 'fracture.i'
    app_type = raccoonApp
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
[]

[Transfers]
  [./disp_x]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_x'
    variable = 'disp_x'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_y'
    variable = 'disp_y'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd_ref'
    variable = 'd_ref'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = from_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd'
    variable = 'd'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./load]
    type = MultiAppScalarToAuxScalarTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'load'
    to_aux_scalar = 'load'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./boundary_xdisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./boundary_ydisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./Periodic]
    [./disp_x]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '1.000000E+01 0 0'
    [../]
    [./disp_y]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '1.000000E+01 0 0'
    [../]
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_film]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_substrate]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+01
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./stress_substrate]
    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_film]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '5.812010E-04'
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_substrate]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '5.812010E+00'
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_film]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 1.000000E-01
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_substrate]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 1.000000E-01
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Postprocessors]
  [./fracture_energy]
    type = FractureEnergy
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = TransientSupNorm
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  dt = 4.927940E-06

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load fracture_energy'
  exodus = true
  print_linear_residuals = false
[]
Close

examples/mud_quasi1D_analytical/script_varying_L_Eratio_200/run0/mechanical.i

[GlobalParams]
  displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = 'geo.msh'
[]

[MultiApps]
  [./fracture]
    type = TransientMultiApp
    input_files = 'fracture.i'
    app_type = raccoonApp
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
[]

[Transfers]
  [./disp_x]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_x'
    variable = 'disp_x'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_y'
    variable = 'disp_y'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd_ref'
    variable = 'd_ref'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = from_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd'
    variable = 'd'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./load]
    type = MultiAppScalarToAuxScalarTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'load'
    to_aux_scalar = 'load'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
[]

  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./boundary_xdisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./boundary_ydisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]

    [./disp_x]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '1.995262E+00 0 0'
    [../]
    [./disp_y]

    block = 'substrate'

  [../]

    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./boundary_xdisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./boundary_ydisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./Periodic]
    [./disp_x]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '3.162278E+00 0 0'
    [../]
    [./disp_y]

      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '3.162278E+00 0 0'
    [../]
  [../]

    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is

    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]

    block = 'substrate'

  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./stress_substrate]
    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'

    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '5.812010E-04'
    block = 'film'

    d = d
  [../]

    block = 'film'
  [../]

examples/mud_quasi1D_analytical/script_varying_L_Eratio_1/run13/mechanical.i

[GlobalParams]
  displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = 'geo.msh'
[]

[MultiApps]
  [./fracture]
    type = TransientMultiApp
    input_files = 'fracture.i'
    app_type = raccoonApp
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
[]

[Transfers]
  [./disp_x]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_x'
    variable = 'disp_x'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_y'
    variable = 'disp_y'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd_ref'
    variable = 'd_ref'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = from_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd'
    variable = 'd'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./load]
    type = MultiAppScalarToAuxScalarTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'load'
    to_aux_scalar = 'load'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./boundary_xdisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./boundary_ydisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./Periodic]
    [./disp_x]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '3.981072E+01 0 0'
    [../]
    [./disp_y]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '3.981072E+01 0 0'
    [../]
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_film]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_substrate]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./stress_substrate]
    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_film]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '4.048456E-04'
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_substrate]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '4.048456E+00'
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_film]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 3.981072E-01
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_substrate]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 3.981072E-01
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
  [../]

    d = d
  [../]

    family = SCALAR
  [../]

    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./boundary_xdisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./boundary_ydisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./Periodic]
    [./disp_x]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '1.000000E+01 0 0'
    [../]
    [./disp_y]

      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '1.000000E+01 0 0'
    [../]
  [../]
[]

    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is

    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]

    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 8.333333E+00
    block = 'substrate'

  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./stress_substrate]
    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]

    type = GenericConstantMaterial

    prop_values = '4.859951E-04'
    block = 'film'

    d = d

    L = 1.000000E-01

    block = 'film'

  [./d]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
  [../]
  [./bounds_dummy]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
[]

[Bounds]
  [./nonnegtivity]
    type = BoundsAux
    variable = bounds_dummy
    bounded_variable = d
    upper = 1
    lower = 0
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./damage]
    type = PhaseFieldFractureEvolution
    variable = d
    driving_energy_name = E_el
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_film]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_substrate]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 2.083333E+00
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./stress_substrate]
    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_film]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.055164E-04'
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_substrate]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.055164E+00'
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_film]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 6.309573E-02
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_substrate]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 6.309573E-02
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -snes_type'
  petsc_options_value = 'lu vinewtonrsls'
  dt = 4.306981E-06

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-06
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false

examples/mud_quasi1D_analytical/script_varying_L_Eratio_20/run10/mechanical.i

[GlobalParams]
  displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = 'geo.msh'
[]

[MultiApps]
  [./fracture]
    type = TransientMultiApp
    input_files = 'fracture.i'
    app_type = raccoonApp
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
[]

[Transfers]
  [./disp_x]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_x'
    variable = 'disp_x'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_y'
    variable = 'disp_y'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd_ref'
    variable = 'd_ref'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = from_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd'
    variable = 'd'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./load]
    type = MultiAppScalarToAuxScalarTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'load'
    to_aux_scalar = 'load'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./boundary_xdisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./boundary_ydisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./Periodic]
    [./disp_x]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '6.309573E+00 0 0'
    [../]
    [./disp_y]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '6.309573E+00 0 0'
    [../]
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_film]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_substrate]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 8.333333E+01
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./stress_substrate]
    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_film]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.973835E-04'
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_substrate]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.973835E+00'
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_film]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 6.309573E-02
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_substrate]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 6.309573E-02
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Postprocessors]
  [./fracture_energy]
    type = FractureEnergy
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = TransientSupNorm
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  dt = 5.776466E-06

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load fracture_energy'
  exodus = true
  print_linear_residuals = false
[]
Close

  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./boundary_xdisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./boundary_ydisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./Periodic]
    [./disp_x]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '3.162278E+01 0 0'
    [../]
    [./disp_y]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '3.162278E+01 0 0'
    [../]
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_film]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_substrate]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 2.083333E+01
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./stress_substrate]

    prop_names = 'b'

    block = 'film'
  [../]

    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_film]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 3.162278E-01
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_substrate]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 3.162278E-01
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
  [../]

  [../]

examples/mud_quasi1D_analytical/script_varying_L_Eratio_0.5/run9/mechanical.i

[GlobalParams]
  displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = 'geo.msh'
[]

[MultiApps]
  [./fracture]
    type = TransientMultiApp
    input_files = 'fracture.i'
    app_type = raccoonApp
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
[]

[Transfers]
  [./disp_x]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_x'
    variable = 'disp_x'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_y'
    variable = 'disp_y'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd_ref'
    variable = 'd_ref'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = from_multiapp

examples/mud_quasi1D_analytical/script_varying_L_Eratio_200/run7/mechanical.i

[GlobalParams]
  displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = 'geo.msh'
[]

[MultiApps]
  [./fracture]
    type = TransientMultiApp
    input_files = 'fracture.i'
    app_type = raccoonApp
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
[]

[Transfers]
  [./disp_x]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_x'
    variable = 'disp_x'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_y'
    variable = 'disp_y'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd_ref'
    variable = 'd_ref'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = from_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd'
    variable = 'd'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./load]
    type = MultiAppScalarToAuxScalarTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'load'
    to_aux_scalar = 'load'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./boundary_xdisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./boundary_ydisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./Periodic]
    [./disp_x]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '4.466836E+00 0 0'
    [../]
    [./disp_y]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '4.466836E+00 0 0'
    [../]
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_film]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_substrate]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 8.333333E+02
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./stress_substrate]
    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_film]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.973835E-04'
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_substrate]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.973835E+00'
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_film]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 4.466836E-02
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_substrate]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 4.466836E-02
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Postprocessors]
  [./fracture_energy]
    type = FractureEnergy
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = TransientSupNorm
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  dt = 5.893127E-06

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  exodus = true
  print_linear_residuals = false

    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'load'
    to_aux_scalar = 'load'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./boundary_xdisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./boundary_ydisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./Periodic]
    [./disp_x]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '5.011872E+00 0 0'
    [../]
    [./disp_y]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '5.011872E+00 0 0'
    [../]
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_film]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_substrate]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 8.333333E+01
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./stress_substrate]
    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_film]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.973835E-04'
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_substrate]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.973835E+00'
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_film]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 5.011872E-02
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_substrate]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 5.011872E-02
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Postprocessors]
  [./fracture_energy]
    type = FractureEnergy
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = TransientSupNorm
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  dt = 5.834601E-06

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  exodus = true

    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_x'
    variable = 'disp_x'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_y'
    variable = 'disp_y'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer

  [../]

    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer

    source_variable = 'd'
    variable = 'd'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]

    type = MultiAppScalarToAuxScalarTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'load'
    to_aux_scalar = 'load'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
[]

[Variables]

  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./boundary_xdisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./boundary_ydisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./Periodic]
    [./disp_x]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '1.995262E+00 0 0'
    [../]
    [./disp_y]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '1.995262E+00 0 0'
    [../]
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_film]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_substrate]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 8.333333E+01
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./stress_substrate]
    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_film]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.973835E-04'
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_substrate]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.973835E+00'
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_film]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 1.995262E-02
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_substrate]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 1.995262E-02
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
  [../]

    type = FractureEnergy
    d = d
  [../]

  petsc_options_value = 'lu'

  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

    component = 1
  [../]

    value = 0
  [../]

    variable = disp_y
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]

      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '3.162278E+01 0 0'
    [../]

      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '3.162278E+01 0 0'
    [../]
  [../]

    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]

    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_substrate]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 2.083333E+00
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./stress_substrate]
    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]

    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.055164E-04'
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_substrate]

    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_film]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 3.162278E-01
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_substrate]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 3.162278E-01
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'substrate'

examples/mud_quasi1D_analytical/script_varying_L_Eratio_5/run5/mechanical.i

[GlobalParams]
  displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = 'geo.msh'
[]

[MultiApps]
  [./fracture]
    type = TransientMultiApp
    input_files = 'fracture.i'
    app_type = raccoonApp
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
[]

[Transfers]
  [./disp_x]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_x'
    variable = 'disp_x'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_y'
    variable = 'disp_y'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd_ref'
    variable = 'd_ref'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = from_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd'
    variable = 'd'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./load]
    type = MultiAppScalarToAuxScalarTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'load'
    to_aux_scalar = 'load'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./boundary_xdisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./boundary_ydisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./Periodic]
    [./disp_x]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '6.309573E+00 0 0'
    [../]
    [./disp_y]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '6.309573E+00 0 0'
    [../]
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_film]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_substrate]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 2.083333E+01
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./stress_substrate]
    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_film]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '5.503124E-04'
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_substrate]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '5.503124E+00'
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_film]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 6.309573E-02
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_substrate]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 6.309573E-02
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Postprocessors]
  [./fracture_energy]
    type = FractureEnergy
    d = d
  [../]

  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

examples/mud_quasi1D_analytical/script_varying_L_Eratio_5/run7/mechanical.i

[GlobalParams]
  displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = 'geo.msh'
[]

[MultiApps]
  [./fracture]
    type = TransientMultiApp
    input_files = 'fracture.i'
    app_type = raccoonApp
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
[]

[Transfers]
  [./disp_x]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_x'
    variable = 'disp_x'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_y'
    variable = 'disp_y'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd_ref'
    variable = 'd_ref'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = from_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd'
    variable = 'd'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./load]
    type = MultiAppScalarToAuxScalarTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'load'
    to_aux_scalar = 'load'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./boundary_xdisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./boundary_ydisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./Periodic]
    [./disp_x]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '1.000000E+01 0 0'
    [../]
    [./disp_y]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '1.000000E+01 0 0'
    [../]
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_film]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_substrate]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 2.083333E+01
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./stress_substrate]
    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_film]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '5.503124E-04'
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_substrate]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '5.503124E+00'
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_film]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 1.000000E-01
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_substrate]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 1.000000E-01
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Postprocessors]
  [./fracture_energy]
    type = FractureEnergy
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = TransientSupNorm
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  dt = 4.798368E-06

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load fracture_energy'
  exodus = true
  print_linear_residuals = false
[]
Close

    [../]

      secondary = 'right'

    [../]
  [../]

    block = 'film'

    block = 'substrate'

    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]

    block = 'film'

    block = 'film'

  [../]

    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit

    [../]

      secondary = 'right'

    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_film]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_substrate]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 8.333333E+00
    block = 'substrate'

  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]

    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'

    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '4.859951E-04'
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_substrate]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '4.859951E+00'
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_film]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 3.981072E-01
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'film'
  [../]

  [../]

    block = 'film'

examples/mud_quasi1D_analytical/script_varying_L_Eratio_200/run9/mechanical.i

[GlobalParams]
  displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = 'geo.msh'
[]

[MultiApps]
  [./fracture]
    type = TransientMultiApp
    input_files = 'fracture.i'
    app_type = raccoonApp
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
[]

[Transfers]
  [./disp_x]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_x'
    variable = 'disp_x'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'disp_y'
    variable = 'disp_y'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd_ref'
    variable = 'd_ref'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./d]
    type = MultiAppCopyTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = from_multiapp
    source_variable = 'd'
    variable = 'd'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
  [./load]
    type = MultiAppScalarToAuxScalarTransfer
    multi_app = fracture
    direction = to_multiapp
    source_variable = 'load'
    to_aux_scalar = 'load'
    execute_on = SAME_AS_MULTIAPP
  [../]
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./d_ref]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./boundary_xdisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./boundary_ydisp]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    boundary = 'bottom'
    value = 0
  [../]
  [./Periodic]
    [./disp_x]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '5.623413E+00 0 0'
    [../]
    [./disp_y]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '5.623413E+00 0 0'
    [../]
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_film]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 4.166667E+00
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor_substrate]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 2.000000E-01
    youngs_modulus = 8.333333E+02
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputeSmallStrain
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress_film]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    history = false
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./stress_substrate]
    type = SmallStrainPK2Stress
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_film]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.973835E-04'
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier_substrate]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3.973835E+00'
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_film]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 5.623413E-02
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'film'
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties_substrate]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8.000000E-04
    L = 5.623413E-02
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
    block = 'substrate'
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Postprocessors]
  [./fracture_energy]
    type = FractureEnergy
    d = d
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = TransientSupNorm
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  dt = 5.797965E-06

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  exodus = true
  print_linear_residuals = false
